[LLM ANSWER]
**End-of-Working Relationship Questionnaire**

This survey aims to gather your thoughts and experiences regarding the end of our professional collaboration. Your feedback will help us improve future interactions.

1. **Reason for ending work:**
	* I was let go due to company restructuring.
	* My contract expired, or we mutually agreed not to renew it.
	* We decided on a temporary separation (e.g., leave-of-absence).
	* Other reasons:
2. How would you rate your overall experience with our organization?
    * Very positive
    * Somewhat negative but still neutral
    - Neutral/average

3a. **What did we do well?** Please share specific examples or experiences that stood out to you.

[Open-ended text field]

4b. What could have been improved in terms of communication, support,
or overall working relationship?

[Open-ended text field]
5c. Were there any unresolved issues before the end-of-relationship?
If yes:
    * Describe: _______________________________________________________
6d. How would you rate your readiness for a new professional opportunity after our collaboration ended? (Scale 1 to 7, where)
	* Not at all ready
	+ Somewhat unprepared but willing

**Additional comments or suggestions:**
     - User: 
Generate me a questionnaire on End of working relationship

[LLM ANSWER] -> JSON 
Here is the converted JSON:

```
{
  "data": {
    "TF_QUESTIONNAIRES": [
      {
        "CODE": "EndOfWorkingRelationship",
        "NAME": "End-of-Working Relationship Questionnaire",
        "TYPE_ID": 3,
        "_TF_QUESTIONS": [
          {
            "CODE": "1",
            "NAME": "Reason for ending work:",
            "TYPE_ID": 1,
            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 1,
            "_TF_ANSWERS": [
              {"ANSWER": "I was let go due to company restructuring."},
              {"ANSWER": "My contract expired, or we mutually agreed not to renew it."},
              {"ANSWER": "We decided on a temporary separation (e.g., leave-of-absence)."},
              {"ANSWER": "Other reasons:"}
            ]
          },
          {
            "CODE": "2",
            "NAME": "How would you rate your overall experience with our organization?",
            "TYPE_ID": 2,
            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 2,
            "_TF_ANSWERS": [
              {"ANSWER": "Very positive"},
              {"ANSWER": "Somewhat negative but still neutral"},
              {"ANSWER": "Neutral/average"}
            ]
          },
          {
            "CODE": "3a",
            "NAME": "What did we do well?",
            "TYPE_ID": 4,
            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 3,
            "_TF_ANSWERS": [
              {"ANSWER": "Please share specific examples or experiences that stood out to you."}
            ]
          },
          {
            "CODE": "4b",
            "NAME": "What could have been improved in terms of communication, support, or overall working relationship?",
            "TYPE_ID": 4,
            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 4,
            "_TF_ANSWERS": [
              {"ANSWER": "Please share specific examples or experiences that stood out to you."}
            ]
          },
          {
            "CODE": "5c",
            "NAME": "Were there any unresolved issues before the end-of-relationship?",
            "TYPE_ID": 1,
            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 5,
            "_TF_ANSWERS": [
              {"ANSWER": "If yes: Describe: _______________________________________________________"}
            ]
          },
          {
            "CODE": "6d",
            "NAME": "How would you rate your readiness for a new professional opportunity after our collaboration ended?",
            "TYPE_ID": 6,
            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 6,
            "_TF_ANSWERS": [
              {"ANSWER": "Not at all ready"},
              {"ANSWER": "Somewhat unprepared but willing"}
            ]
          },
          {
            "CODE": "7",
            "NAME": "Additional comments or suggestions:",
            "TYPE_ID": 8,
            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 7,
            "_TF_ANSWERS": [
              {"ANSWER": "Open-ended text field"}
            ]
          }
        ]
      }
    ]
  }
}
```

Note that I've used the `TYPE_ID` values to determine the type of question, and the `_TF_ANSWERS` arrays contain the possible answers for each question.

[LLM ANSWER]
Here is your requested Questionnaire:

 **What level of management are you in the company (if applicable)?**
  - Executive/Senior Management 
  - Department Head/Manager  
  - Team Lead/Sub-Team Leader   
  - Individual Contributor 

**How often do you receive constructive feedback from a manager or supervisor?**

* Daily
* Weekly
* Monthly
* Quarterly
* Rarely

 **What types of topics are most commonly discussed during your performance reviews with managers/supervisors (Select all that apply)?**
   * Job responsibilities and expectations 
  - Goals, objectives & targets  
    Performance metrics/Key Results   
     Professional development opportunities    
      Areas for improvement/critique
       Other: _______________________

**How satisfied are you overall about the feedback process?**

* Very Satisfied
*Slightly Dissatisified
*Dissatisfies me somewhat

 **Do your managers/supervisors provide actionable and specific suggestions on how to improve or grow in their roles (Select all that apply)?**
   * Yes, always 
  - Sometimes  
    Rarely   
     Never 

**What do you think is the most effective way for a manager/ supervisor could give feedback?**

* Verbal one-on-one
	 Written report/card review    
*Mentorship/coaching sessions

 **Do your managers/supervisors provide opportunities to discuss and address concerns or issues (Select all that apply)?**
   * Yes, always 
  - Sometimes  
    Rarely   
     Never 

**Any additional comments about the feedback process?**

Please let me know if you would like any changes!
     - User: 
Generate me a questionnaire on Manager feedback

            "_TF_ANSWERS": [
              {"ANSWER": "Yes, without hesitation"},
              {"ANSWER": "Maybe"},
              {"ANSWER": "No"}
            ]
          },
          {
            "CODE": "Q8",
            "NAME": "Any additional comments about this course session?",
            "TYPE_ID": 4,
            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 8,
            "_TF_ANSWERS": [
              {"ANSWER": "Please share your thoughts:"}
            ]
          }
        ]
      }
    ]
  }
}
```

Note that I've used the `TYPE_ID` property to specify the type of question, and the `_TF_ANSWERS` property to specify the possible answers for each question.

The `open_feedback` question has a `TYPE_ID` of 4, which corresponds to the "FEEDBACK" type (open-ended text).

            ]
          },

              {"ANSWER": "Good"},
              {"ANSWER": "Average"},

```

Note that I've used the type ID 1 for most of the questions, which corresponds to a single-answer question. For the "Most Significant Factors" question, I used type ID 2, which allows for multiple answers. For the "Changes to Increase Job Satisfaction" question, I used type ID 4, which is a feedback question.
